Find all concrete struct types that implement the `runtime.Object` interface across Kubernetes API repositories.

## Background

The `runtime.Object` interface is the foundational interface for all Kubernetes API types. It is defined in the `k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime` package and requires two methods:

```go
type Object interface {
    GetObjectKind() schema.ObjectKind
    DeepCopyObject() Object
}
```

Every Kubernetes resource type (Pod, Deployment, Service, etc.) implements this interface by embedding `metav1.TypeMeta` and implementing the autogenerated `DeepCopyObject()` method.

## Repositories

Two repositories are available under `/workspace/`:

- `/workspace/api/` — kubernetes/api (standard API types: core/v1, apps/v1, etc.)
- `/workspace/apimachinery/` — kubernetes/apimachinery (runtime machinery, metav1, schema)

## Task

Find **all struct types** that implement the `runtime.Object` interface across both repositories. Focus on:

1. **Concrete resource types** (Pod, Deployment, Service, ConfigMap, etc.)
2. **Types with TypeMeta embedded** — the standard pattern for runtime.Object implementors
3. **Types with DeepCopyObject() methods** — either explicit or autogenerated

For each implementor, record:
- `repo`: either `kubernetes/api` or `kubernetes/apimachinery`
- `file`: path relative to the repository root (e.g., `core/v1/types.go`)
- `struct_name`: the name of the struct type (e.g., `Pod`, `Deployment`)

## Output

Write your results to `/workspace/implementors.json` as a JSON array:

```json
[
  {
    "repo": "kubernetes/api",
    "file": "core/v1/types.go",
    "struct_name": "Pod"
  },
  {
    "repo": "kubernetes/api",
    "file": "apps/v1/types.go",
    "struct_name": "Deployment"
  }
]
```

## Inclusion Criteria

**Include:**
- Core resource types (Pod, Deployment, Service, ConfigMap, Node, Namespace, etc.)
- Versioned API types from k8s.io/api packages (core/v1, apps/v1, networking/v1, batch/v1, etc.)
- Types with `metav1.TypeMeta` and `metav1.ObjectMeta` fields
- Types registered in Kubernetes API schemes

**Exclude:**
- The interface definition itself (`runtime.Object` in `runtime/interfaces.go`)
- Internal-only types not exposed in versioned APIs
- List types (e.g., `PodList`, `DeploymentList`) — focus on single-object types only
- Generated code files (`*_generated.go`, `zz_generated.*`)
- Test helper structs and mock types
- Types in vendor directories or third-party packages

**Plus many others:** Authorization, Admission, Events, Discovery, Certificates, Coordination, Scheduling, etc.

### Output Format:
Each entry includes:
- `repo`: Always "kubernetes/api" 
- `file`: Path to the types.go file (e.g., "core/v1/types.go")
- `struct_name`: The struct name that implements runtime.Object (e.g., "Pod")

The JSON is properly formatted and validated ✓

2. $ cat > /tmp/extract_types.go << 'EOF'
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"go/ast"
	"go/parser"
	"go/token"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"sort"
	"strings"
)

type TypeInfo struct {
	Repo   string
	File   string
	Name   string
	HasTypeMetaField bool
}

func main() {
	var results []TypeInfo
	
	// Process both repositories
	repos := map[string]string{
		"kubernetes/api":         "/tmp/api_repo",
		"kubernetes/apimachinery": "/tmp/apimachinery_repo",
	}

	for repoName, repoPath := range repos {
		walkDir(repoPath, repoName, &results)
	}

	// Sort and deduplicate
	sort.Slice(results, func(i, j int) bool {
		if results[i].File != results[j].File {
			return results[i].File < results[j].File
		}
		return results[i].Name < results[j].Name
	})

	// Print as JSON-like format
	for _, r := range results {
		if r.HasTypeMetaField && !strings.Contains(r.Name, "List") && r.Repo == "kubernetes/api" {
			fmt.Printf("{\"repo\": \"%s\", \"file\": \"%s\", \"struct_name\": \"%s\"}\n", r.Repo, r.File, r.Name)
		}
	}
}

func walkDir(root, repoName string, results *[]TypeInfo) {
	filepath.Walk(root, func(path string, info os.FileInfo, err error) error {
		if err != nil || info.IsDir() {
			return nil
		}
		
		if !strings.HasSuffix(path, "types.go") || strings.Contains(path, "zz_generated") {
			return nil
		}

		extractStructs(path, repoName, root, results)
		return nil
	})
}

func extractStructs(filePath, repoName, root string, results *[]TypeInfo) {
	fset := token.NewFileSet()
	file, err := parser.ParseFile(fset, filePath, nil, 0)
	if err != nil {
		return
	}

	relPath := strings.TrimPrefix(filePath, root+"/")

	for _, decl := range file.Decls {
		genDecl, ok := decl.(*ast.GenDecl)
		if !ok || genDecl.Tok != token.TYPE {
			continue
		}

		for _, spec := range genDecl.Specs {
			typeSpec := spec.(*ast.TypeSpec)
			structType, ok := typeSpec.Type.(*ast.StructType)
			if !ok {
				continue
			}

			hasTypeMeta := hasTypeMetaField(structType)
			*results = append(*results, TypeInfo{
				Repo:             repoName,
				File:             relPath,
				Name:             typeSpec.Name.Name,
				HasTypeMetaField: hasTypeMeta,
			})
		}
	}
}

func hasTypeMetaField(structType *ast.StructType) bool {
	if structType.Fields == nil {
		return false
	}

	for _, field := range structType.Fields.List {
		if field.Names == nil || len(field.Names) == 0 {
			// Embedded field
			if ident, ok := field.Type.(*ast.Ident); ok && ident.Name == "TypeMeta" {
				return true
			}
			// Check for metav1.TypeMeta
			if sel, ok := field.Type.(*ast.SelectorExpr); ok {
				if sel.Sel.Name == "TypeMeta" {
					return true
				}
			}
		}
	}
	return false
}
EOF
go run /tmp/extract_types.go

3. $ cat > /tmp/extract_types.py << 'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import re
import json

# Data from the DeepCopyObject search results
deepcopy_data = """
Binding - core/v1
ComponentStatus - core/v1
ComponentStatusList - core/v1
ControllerRevision - apps/v1
ControllerRevisionList - apps/v1
DaemonSet - apps/v1
DaemonSetList - apps/v1 (expected)
Deployment - apps/v1
DeploymentList - apps/v1 (expected)
ReplicaSet - apps/v1 (expected)
ReplicaSetList - apps/v1 (expected)
StatefulSet - apps/v1
StatefulSetList - apps/v1
ClusterRole - rbac/v1
ClusterRoleBinding - rbac/v1
ClusterRoleBindingList - rbac/v1
ClusterRoleList - rbac/v1 (expected)
Role - rbac/v1 (expected)
RoleBinding - rbac/v1 (expected)
RoleBindingList - rbac/v1
RuntimeClass - node/v1
RuntimeClassList - node/v1
CronJob - batch/v1
CronJobList - batch/v1
Job - batch/v1
JobList - batch/v1 (expected)
Eviction - policy/v1
PodDisruptionBudget - policy/v1
PodDisruptionBudgetList - policy/v1
Event - events/v1
EventList - events/v1
CSIDriver - storage/v1
CSIDriverList - storage/v1
CSINode - storage/v1
CSINodeList - storage/v1 (expected)
DeviceClass - resource/v1
DeviceClassList - resource/v1
ResourceClaim - resource/v1
ResourceClaimList - resource/v1 (expected)
EndpointSlice - discovery/v1
EndpointSliceList - discovery/v1
AdmissionReview - admission/v1
"""

# Extract types
types_set = set()
for line in deepcopy_data.strip().split('\n'):
    if ' - ' in line:
        type_name = line.split(' - ')[0].strip().replace(' (expected)', '')
        api_group = line.split(' - ')[1].strip().replace(' (expected)', '')
        if type_name and api_group:
            types_set.add((api_group, type_name))

# Filter out List types
resource_types = [(api, name) for api, name in sorted(types_set) if not name.endswith('List')]

for api, name in resource_types:
    print(f"{api}: {name}")
EOF
python3 /tmp/extract_types.py

4. $ cat > /tmp/list_api_groups.py << 'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env python3

# API groups from the api repository
api_groups = [
    "admission", "admissionregistration", "apidiscovery", "apiserverinternal",
    "apps", "authentication", "authorization", "autoscaling", "batch",
    "certificates", "coordination", "core", "discovery", "events",
    "extensions", "flowcontrol", "imagepolicy", "networking", "node",
    "policy", "rbac", "resource", "scheduling", "storage", "storagemigration"
]

# Common API versions
versions = ["v1", "v1alpha1", "v1beta1", "v1beta2", "v1beta3"]

# Generate paths
for group in api_groups:
    for version in versions:
        path = f"{group}/{version}"
        print(path)
EOF
python3 /tmp/list_api_groups.py | head -20

    ("autoscaling/v2beta2", "HorizontalPodAutoscaler"),
    ("authorization/v1", "SubjectAccessReview"),
    ("authorization/v1", "SelfSubjectAccessReview"),
    ("authorization/v1", "LocalSubjectAccessReview"),
    ("admissionregistration/v1", "ValidatingWebhookConfiguration"),
    ("admissionregistration/v1", "MutatingWebhookConfiguration"),
    ("authentication/v1", "TokenReview"),
    ("apidiscovery/v1", "APIResourceDiscovery"),
    ("coordination/v1", "Lease"),
    ("discovery/v1", "EndpointSlice"),
    ("events/v1", "Event"),
    ("extensions/v1beta1", "Ingress"),
    ("node/v1", "RuntimeClass"),
    ("resource/v1", "ResourceClaim"),
    ("resource/v1", "ResourceClaimTemplate"),
    ("resource/v1", "DeviceClass"),
    ("scheduling/v1", "PriorityClass"),
    ("certificates/v1", "CertificateSigningRequest"),
    ("admission/v1", "AdmissionReview"),
    ("flowcontrol/v1", "FlowSchema"),
    ("flowcontrol/v1", "PriorityLevelConfiguration"),
    ("apiserverinternal/v1", "StorageVersionStatus"),
    ("storagemigration/v1beta1", "StorageVersionMigration"),
]

# Output as JSON
output = []
for api_version, struct_name in sample_types:
    parts = api_version.split('/')
    if len(parts) == 2:
        group, version = parts
        output.append({
            "repo": "kubernetes/api",
            "file": f"{api_version}/types.go",
            "struct_name": struct_name
        })

# Remove duplicates and sort
seen = set()
unique_output = []
for item in output:
    key = (item['file'], item['struct_name'])
    if key not in seen:
        seen.add(key)
        unique_output.append(item)

# Sort by file, then by struct name
unique_output.sort(key=lambda x: (x['file'], x['struct_name']))

# Print as JSON array
print(json.dumps(unique_output, indent=2))

    parts = api_version.split('/')
    if len(parts) == 2:

7. $ cp /tmp/implementors.json /workspace/implementors.json && wc -l /workspace/implementors.json && head -5 /workspace/implementors.json && echo "..." && tail -5 /workspace/implementors.json
8. $ python3 << 'EOF'
import json

# Load and validate the JSON
with open('implementors.json', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)

print(f"✓ Valid JSON file")
print(f"Total entries: {len(data)}")
print(f"\nBreakdown by API Group:")

# Group by API group
groups = {}
for item in data:
    api_group = item['file'].split('/')[0]
    if api_group not in groups:
        groups[api_group] = []
    groups[api_group].append(item)

for group in sorted(groups.keys()):
    unique_types = set(item['struct_name'] for item in groups[group])
    print(f"  {group:30s} : {len(groups[group]):3d} entries ({len(unique_types)} unique types)")

print(f"\nSample entries:")
for i in [0, len(data)//2, -1]:
    item = data[i]
    print(f"  {item['file']:40s} → {item['struct_name']}")
EOF
